             <a href="https://www.nbcnews.com/health/health-news/plan-your-vaccine-everything-you-need-know-about-getting-covid-n1257438">
              <span>
               Plan Your Vaccine
              </span>
             </a>
            </h2>
           </div>
           <div class="tease-card__info" data-test="tease-card__info">
            <h2 class="tease-card__headline tease-card__title relative">
             <a href="https://www.nbcnews.com/specials/plan-your-vaccine/">
              <span class="tease-card__headline">
               Everything you need to know about getting a Covid-19 vaccination
              </span>
             </a>
             <span class="">
             </span>
            </h2>
            <p class="dek tease-card__dek">
             NBC News has designed a tool that tells you everything you need to know about getting a Covid-19 shot, based on your unique situation. Plan your own vaccine — or help a loved one.
            </p>
